data-css=tve-u-17724e3dc87><p>Before using Cash App for sending and receiving money, it’s important to be aware of Cash App’s customer service, including the contact information, reviews, ratings, and complaints listed below.<h2>Cash App Customer Service Reviews and Complaints</h2><p>When considering using Cash App for peer-to-peer payments, investing, or managing your finances, it’s helpful to review Cash App customer service reviews and complaints. Cash App, developed by Square Inc., is a popular mobile payment service that allows users to send and receive money, buy Bitcoin, and invest in stocks. Cash App has received various feedback from users regarding their support and service. Reviews often highlight the convenience of sending money, the ease of setting up an account, and the additional features like investing and Cash Boost discounts, while some complaints focus on issues like account security, fraudulent transactions, and customer support responsiveness. Comparing Cash App with competitors like <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/venmo-customer-service/>Venmo</a>, <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/paypal-customer-service/>PayPal</a>, and <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/zelle/>Zelle</a> can provide a broader perspective on customer service experiences in the mobile payment industry.<p>Other competition in the banking industry Includes <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/bankmobile/>BankMobile</a>, <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/ally-bank-phone-number/>Ally Bank</a>, <a href=https://customerservicenumbers.com/dave-customer-service/>Dave</a>.<h3>How to Contact Cash App</h3><p>To contact Cash App, you can use the following information:<ul><li><strong>General Customer Service:</strong> <a href=tel:1-800-969-1940>1-800-969-1940</a><li><strong>Support via App:</strong> Open Cash App > Tap the profile icon > Select “Support” > Tap “Something Else” > Choose your issue and tap “Contact Support”<li><strong>Customer Service Hours:</strong> Available 24/7 through the app and online help center<li><strong>Corporate Office Address:</strong> Cash App (Square Inc.), 1455 Market Street, Suite 600, San Francisco, CA 94103<li><strong>Website:</strong> <a href=https://cash.app target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer">cash.app</a></ul><p>At CustomerServiceNumbers.com, we also provide a rating and comment section where you can leave your own review. Evaluating these reviews and complaints can help you make an informed decision about using Cash App for your payment and financial needs.<p><strong>Note:</strong> This website listing is not associated with Cash App or Square Inc. The information and the reviews are a service provided by CustomerServiceNumbers.com.<p>Cash App does not provide support services directly through this website.
